CREATE DATABASE /*!32312 IF NOT EXISTS*/`educate` /*!40100 DEFAULT CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci */;

USE `educate`;

/*Table structure for table `category` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `category`;

CREATE TABLE `category` (
  `category_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `category_name` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`category_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Data for the table `category` */

(5,'Google Cloud'),
(6,'Linux'),
(7,'Security');

/*Table structure for table `course` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `course`;

CREATE TABLE `course` (
  `category_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `course_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `course_name` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  `course_duration` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`course_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=44 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Table structure for table `course_schedule` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `course_schedule`;

CREATE TABLE `course_schedule` (
  `schedule_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `schedule_name` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `course_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `start_date` date NOT NULL,
  `input_monday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_tuesday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_wednesday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_thursday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_friday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_saturday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `input_sunday` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `done_percent` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `all_duration` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`,`course_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Data for the table `course_schedule` */

insert  into `course_schedule`(`schedule_id`,`schedule_name`,`user_id`,`course_id`,`start_date`,`input_monday`,`input_tuesday`,`input_wednesday`,`input_thursday`,`input_friday`,`input_saturday`,`input_sunday`,`end_date`,`done_percent`,`all_duration`) values 
(1,'123',0,2,'2021-01-14',0,0,0,0,0,0,1,'2021-06-20','4.18%','74831'),
(1,'xxx472',0,29,'2021-01-14',0.5,0.5,1.5,2.5,0.5,0.5,0.5,'2021-01-22','0.00%','31456'),
(1,'asss',0,34,'2021-01-14',0,0,1,0,0,0,0,'2021-01-20','0.00%','11533');

/*Table structure for table `discuss` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `discuss`;

CREATE TABLE `discuss` (
  `video_path_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `user_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `content` varchar(1000) NOT NULL,
  `discuss_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`video_path_id`,`discuss_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Data for the table `discuss` */

/*Table structure for table `section` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `section`;

CREATE TABLE `section` (
  `course_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `section_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `section_name` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  `section_duration` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`section_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=575 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Table structure for table `sequence` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `sequence`;

CREATE TABLE `sequence` (
  `seq_name` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `current_val` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `increment_val` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`seq_name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

/*Data for the table `sequence` */

insert  into `sequence`(`seq_name`,`current_val`,`increment_val`) values 
('category_id',7,1),
('course_id',43,1),
('download_id',0,1),
('section_id',574,1),
('video_id',3279,1);

/*Table structure for table `user` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `user`;

CREATE TABLE `user` (
  `status` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `user_name` char(100) NOT NULL,
  `password` char(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`status`,`user_id`,`user_name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Data for the table `user` */

insert  into `user`(`status`,`user_id`,`user_name`,`password`) values 
(0,0,'liming','234567'),
(1,0,'wangping','123456');

/*Table structure for table `user_records` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `user_records`;

CREATE TABLE `user_records` (
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `video_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `done_flg` int(10) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`video_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Data for the table `user_records` */

/*Table structure for table `video` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `video`;

CREATE TABLE `video` (
  `section_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `video_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `video_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `video_path` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  `video_duration` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`video_id`),
  KEY `video_id` (`video_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=3280 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Table structure for table `video_schedule` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `video_schedule`;

CREATE TABLE `video_schedule` (
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `course_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `video_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `plan_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `overlay_flg` int(10) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`,`course_id`,`video_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/* Function  structure for function  `currentValue` */

/*!50003 DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS `currentValue` */;
DELIMITER $$

/*!50003 CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`%` FUNCTION `currentValue`(v_seq_name VARCHAR(50)) RETURNS int(11)
BEGIN
	DECLARE VALUE INTEGER;
	SET VALUE = 0;
	SELECT current_val INTO VALUE  FROM sequence WHERE seq_name = v_seq_name;
	RETURN VALUE;
    END */$$
DELIMITER ;

/* Function  structure for function  `nextValue` */

/*!50003 DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS `nextValue` */;
DELIMITER $$

/*!50003 CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`%` FUNCTION `nextValue`(v_seq_name VARCHAR(50)) RETURNS int(11)
BEGIN
	UPDATE sequence SET current_val = current_val + increment_val  WHERE seq_name = v_seq_name;
	RETURN currentValue(v_seq_name);
    END */$$
DELIMITER ;
